#.Cider.Cider.ChangeCurrentDir — 19%↟‚ÜĎ
{r}‚Üź{dry}ChangeCurrentDir path [1] ‚ćĚ Might change the current directory. [2] ‚ćĚ First condition is that the current project is the first one opened in the WS. [3] ‚ćĚ If that's the case then the current dir is changed to the project's dir if Cider's global config file [4] ‚ćĚ does not carry an entry `GetGlobalAskForDirChange`. #.Cider.Cider.InjectTatinVars — 88%↟‚ÜĎ
ref‚ÜźInjectTatinVars(projectRoot folder) [1] ‚ćĚ When a package is loaded, a namespace `TatinVars` is injected into the root of the package by Tatin. [2] ‚ćĚ When Cider opens a project that carries a file apl-package.json in the projects's root folder, it [3] ‚ćĚ injects such a namespace in the root of the project by default.\\ [4] ‚ćĚ However, more often than not a sub-namespace of the project will eventually become the package. [5] ‚ćĚ In such a case you might want to have `TatinVars` in the root of the _**package**_ namespace.\\ [6] ‚ćĚ You can achieve that by injecting a property `tatinVars` into the Cider config file (as part of [7] ‚ćĚ `CONFIG`) in order to specify a sub-namespace that will eventually become the package. [8] ‚ćĚ Cider will then inject `TatinVars` into that sub-namespace rather than the root of the project, [9] ‚ćĚ This allows a developer to access `TatinVars` while working on the project as if it were loaded [10] ‚ćĚ as a package.\\ [11] ‚ćĚ `ref‚Üź‚éēNULL` if the project does not have a package config file and a ref to `TatinVars` otherwise. [12] ‚ćĚ point to a sub-namespace in the project's root.
